Multiple configurations for devices which can be woken can be created. For each configuration a live tile can be made.\r\n\r\nSome simple explanation on WOL. Some devices support sleep/hibernate modes where the device (PC, etc) can be woken by a so-called magic packet on the ethernet (or wireless) interface. This tool can send this magic packet.
